Telehealth & Jane Payments
As a little bit of background, our
integrated payment
partner, Stripe, has telehealth listed as a â€œrestrictedâ€ service (which is not the same as prohibited). This is pretty standard in the payments industry since telehealth is deemed as â€˜higher riskâ€™ for folks selling illegal products or services. And, while that might make sense in the payment processing world, we know it doesnâ€™t for our customers, who are using telehealth to provide care for their communities.
So weâ€™veÂ beenÂ working closely with Stripe to find a solution and
Iâ€™m happy to say that Jane users who offer telehealth will no longer have to fill out any additional documentation! ðŸŽ‰
A quick note about
telemedicine
: Stripeâ€™s terms of service (like most other payment solutions) prohibit the sale of prescription medications, including via a video call. So
if you prescribe and use telehealth
, you may still have your account paused while Stripe requests more information.
If youâ€™re curious if this would apply to your business, please

to chat. ðŸ’™

Changelog: January 23rd, 2023
Improved PCI Compliance
If youâ€™re not familiar with
PCI Compliance
, itâ€™s a standard to ensure business owners are maintaining safe payments for their clients, including proper storage of credit card information.
Jane is a secure platform for storing clientsâ€™ data, but it can still be used in ways that are not PCI-compliant, like collecting and storing credit card numbers in plain text in chart entries.
To help you maintain compliance, weâ€™ll be
removing the ability to record credit card information in charting fields
(
including Intake Forms
) by
January 31st.
ðŸ“†Â Similar to other note fields in Jane, any 16-digit number will be replaced with stars once saved.
ðŸŽ‰
Jane Payments
is PCI compliant
and allows you to easily collect and store credit card info in three ways:
Collect Credit Cards through Online Booking
Collect Credit Cards on Intake Forms
Collect Credit Cards using the Jane Payments Terminal
If youâ€™re not using Jane Payments yet, it only takes 5 minutes
to get set up

reach out
if you have any questions!

Telehealth & Jane Payments
As a little bit of background, our
integrated payment
partner, Stripe, has telehealth listed as a â€œrestrictedâ€ service (which is not the same as prohibited). This is pretty standard in the payments industry since telehealth is deemed as â€˜higher riskâ€™ for folks selling illegal products or services. And, while that might make sense in the payment processing world, we know it doesnâ€™t for our customers, who are using telehealth to provide care for their communities.
So weâ€™veÂ beenÂ working closely with Stripe to find a solution and
Iâ€™m happy to say that Jane users who offer telehealth will no longer have to fill out any additional documentation! ðŸŽ‰
A quick note about
telemedicine
: Stripeâ€™s terms of service (like most other payment solutions) prohibit the sale of prescription medications, including via a video call. So
if you prescribe and use telehealth
, you may still have your account paused while Stripe requests more information.
If youâ€™re curious if this would apply to your business, please

to chat. ðŸ’™

Changelog: January 23rd, 2023
Improved PCI Compliance
If youâ€™re not familiar with
PCI Compliance
, itâ€™s a standard to ensure business owners are maintaining safe payments for their clients, including proper storage of credit card information.
Jane is a secure platform for storing clientsâ€™ data, but it can still be used in ways that are not PCI-compliant, like collecting and storing credit card numbers in plain text in chart entries.
To help you maintain compliance, weâ€™ll be
removing the ability to record credit card information in charting fields

Changelog: May 30th, 2022
Update: Jane Payments Cut-Off Time
The new cutoff time for
Jane Payments
is 11:59 pm ET / 8:59 pm PT.
ðŸŽ‰
This means that all payments processed before 11:59 pm for our East Coasters and 8:59 pm for those of us out West will be deposited into your account at the same time. Say goodbye to having payments from the same calendar day split into two deposits on two separate days! We hope this helps make your bookkeeping a little easier.

Changelog: October 8th, 2021
